Current Commentary

The Tragic Fire on Avenue Edward VII 28

— Ting

Shanghai is densely populated, with houses clustered together. In the event of a fire, it easily becomes a disaster. The sacrifice of lives and the loss of property are both substantial. In recent years, the municipal authorities in various districts have recognized this and have strived to improve fire prevention facilities. Taking the First Special District (International Settlement) as an example, the percentage of disaster losses in the district over the past twenty years has decreased from 40% in 1908 to 0.99% in 1933. The difference between the two is vast, which cannot be said to be insignificant progress. However, incidents such as the carelessness at the Zhengtai Rubber Factory on Tangshan Road on February 21st last year, which killed 81 people and injured 50, and the fire at the Ni Shunxing cotton shop on Avenue Edward VII yesterday morning, which killed 14 people and injured over 20, are still horrifying tragedies. This is a very serious social problem today and is closely related to the interests of all citizens.

Analyzing the causes of fires over the years, focusing on the special environment of Shanghai, we can identify the following three points.

(1) Overcrowding in Ordinary Residences: Housing in Shanghai is expensive, and those with middle-class incomes or lower often lament, "It is difficult to live in a big city." Even a single-story new house, with an upper and lower level, can cost as much as 70 yuan per month in rent. This inevitably leads to overcrowding. On average, six families live in an ordinary city house. The Du family's cotton shop, which was hit by the fire yesterday, housed eight families. The living quarters were nearly full, including the reception hall, back kitchen, front building, back building, attic, front attic, and back attic. Dozens of people lived, rested, ate, and relieved themselves in this small space. It goes without saying that this is detrimental to hygiene, and with so many people, disasters are more likely to occur. Once a disaster strikes suddenly, even in broad daylight, it is difficult to escape one by one. Moreover, since it occurred at 4 AM, survival was unlikely.

(2) Lack of Disaster Relief Knowledge: Among the more than three million citizens of Shanghai, only a small minority have knowledge and experience in fire prevention and disaster relief. If they unfortunately encounter a severe fire and lack external assistance, they can only wait to die. For example, among the residents of the First Special District who died in fires last year, there were 93 people. All 93 of these people died before the firefighters arrived. If people cannot save themselves, let alone save others, they are destined to perish together in the event of an accident. This is the reality, both pitiful and lamentable.

(3) Lack of Firefighting Equipment: Ordinary residences in the city are cramped and crowded, with little room to maneuver, and firefighting equipment is even more lacking. Landlords treat fire insurance policies as talismans, considering them unnecessary, while tenants who are just trying to make a living have no energy or resources to pay attention to this. The latest firefighting equipment is expensive, which may be impractical. However, the installation of simple things like fire extinguishing chemicals and fire hoses is easy to do, but they are completely lacking due to short-sightedness, laziness, and ingrained habits that are difficult to change. This is truly like the saying, "Swallows living in a hall think they are safe, but they do not know that the building is about to burn down."

To address this issue, we must: (1) The municipal authorities should strictly crack down on the abuses of "second landlords" who subdivide houses and charge exorbitant rents. The prerequisite is to stabilize the rise in general rents. (2) The work of building inspections and fire prevention, if it has been effective, must be gradually expanded in scope, and the methods must be stricter. Attention should be paid to the residential areas of the lower middle class and the factory areas. In the First Special District, areas such as Hongkou and Yangshupu have frequent fires and should be the focus of future efforts. (3) Arouse the public's interest in fire prevention and disaster relief. In early August of this year, the Shanghai County Farmers' Education Center held a fire drill in Zhuanqiao Town, which was very successful and can be promoted in a similar way. In Europe and the United States, there is an annual "Fire Prevention Day," during which everyone is excited and participates in activities, inspecting their homes or cleaning their residences. If they find anything that could cause danger, they remove it immediately without hesitation. Even a small match is carefully placed. This contains a very good intention and is of great value for us to imitate.

Impact of Silver Tax Collection on the International Scene: Comments from the London Financial News 29

(Washington) The State Department has no criticism of China's imposition of an export tax on silver today. Responsible parties believe that the U.S. response is merely lip service. It is interpreted here that Secretary of State Hull repeatedly discussed the matter with Secretary of the Treasury Morgenthau before issuing the response because the Treasury Department was unwilling to prevent the rise in silver prices. The actions taken by China now put the U.S. government in a difficult position. On the one hand, the silver lobby is seeking to raise prices quickly before the congressional elections, while on the other hand, the friendship and prosperity of China are also seen as necessary for the government's commercial policy. (14th National News Agency Dispatch)

(London) A major bullion broker told a Reuters reporter today that China has been forced by the U.S. silver policy and is now managing its silver reserves. The current tax rate should not be regarded as final. He believes that if the market price skyrockets, the tax rate will continue to increase, willing to make any sacrifice to maintain its main policy. China has now separated from the world and does not need to be forced to implement austerity measures to resist the currency exchange situation in the Far East caused by U.S. purchases. Any increase in the world silver price will enable China to implement austerity measures because the value of its silver reserves can increase due to the rise in world prices. He believes that there will be two silver prices in the future, one for China and one for the world. All major brokers believe that the continuous outflow of silver from China recently has forced the Chinese government to come up with this plan. Speculators now see China's increased silver tax as beneficial in many ways because China will no longer sell large quantities of silver in the future. However, another expert said that Chinese banks with silver deposits abroad can still sell them continuously because they can make quick profits. However, the current silver market is entirely controlled by speculators, so the future trend is extremely difficult to predict. (15th Reuters Dispatch)

Bombay: It is generally believed that the Chinese government's preparation to collect silver export tax is beneficial in many ways. The U.S. attitude has not changed yet. Local merchants are now watching the trend in London. The Bombay silver market did not open this morning because of a dispute between brokers and merchants over brokerage fees. It did not resume normal business until 2 PM. The silver price was 15 annas higher than the closing price on Saturday. (15th Reuters News Agency Dispatch)

(London) The "Financial News" editorial today, discussing the effects of the U.S. silver policy, stated briefly: "China's protest against the U.S. silver policy has attracted the attention of the United States. In the future, the U.S. authorities will obviously take appropriate measures to purchase silver to avoid the improper absorption of other countries' reserves. However, it is clear that the U.S. silver purchase plan will continue. As for China, which is in a crisis of currency contraction due to the outflow of silver, it has now decided to impose a heavy tax on silver exports in order to cope with the situation. As a result, the price of silver will inevitably continue to rise. After China imposes a tax on silver exports, the U.S. demand for silver will not be affected, but the main source of silver supply will be greatly reduced. In this case, how can one expect the silver price not to continue to rise?" (15th Havas News Agency Dispatch)

U.S. Plans to Open Air Route Across the Pacific 35

Directly to the Far East via Hawaii

Cooperation with China National Aviation Corporation

(Washington) Juan Trippe, manager of Pan American Airways, wrote to Postmaster General Farley today, stating that the final plan for the Pacific air route from the United States to the Far East is now being prepared. On the American side, this route will connect with Pan American's air route in Central and South America, and on the Far East side, it will cooperate with the Sino-American-operated China National Aviation Corporation. Trippe said that Charles Lindbergh is currently leading the company's technical personnel to study whether the climate on the U.S. West Coast is suitable for opening the eastern terminus of the new air route. The company has also selected aircraft for use in the opening. The first flight will use a four-engine aircraft with a speed of 191 miles per hour. It is planned to conduct a test flight as soon as possible. Postmaster General Farley replied with great approval and predicted that both commercial and international relations would benefit. Trippe continued that the new route will pass through Hawaii, Guam, and the Philippine Islands. After opening, four-engine Sikorsky amphibious aircraft will fly from California to China, a journey of three days. The aircraft can accommodate 32 passengers. It is reported that China National Aviation Corporation also plans to resume the Shanghai-Hong Kong route in a few weeks, and the Hong Kong-Manila air route will be opened after the Pacific air route is realized. Laval Inherits His Predecessor's Legacy; French Foreign Policy Remains Unchanged 45

Important Meeting Between French and Czech Foreign Ministers

Renier Resigns as Minister of Justice

(Berlin) The future of relations between Germany and France is significant, so Germany must pay close attention to the successor of the French Foreign Minister. The new French Foreign Minister, Laval, was born in Chateldon, Auvergne, in 1883. Laval's family was poor, and the people of that region are known for their fortitude and perseverance, so Laval also possesses those traits. Most French politicians are familiar with the law, so Laval also practiced law. In 1914, he was first elected as a member of parliament, but he lost the election in 1919. He re-entered parliament in 1924 as a member of the Independent Socialist Party and also served as the mayor of Aubervilliers, a position he still holds. Laval joined Briand's cabinet in 1926 as Minister of Justice and later served as ministers in various cabinet departments. He resigned in 1931 and formed his own cabinet. In the autumn of that year, the global economic crisis began, and Laval and Foreign Minister Briand visited Germany together, the first time a French Prime Minister had visited Germany. Laval is now a member of the Senate but does not belong to any political party. It is said that his foreign policy will follow in the footsteps of Barthou and will not be changed. Landin, the successor to Laval as Colonial Minister, was born in 1879 and also practiced law. He has been a member of parliament since 1919 and has held important positions in the cabinet. (14th National Telegram)

Benes then met with Foreign Minister Laval and will continue talks tomorrow morning. Benes is one of the important diplomats of the Little Entente countries, and the discussions are likely to be related to the situation after the assassination of the King of Yugoslavia. (15th Havas Telegram)

However, the successor to Minister of Justice Chéron after his resignation has not yet been determined. Renier was unwilling to accept the position and asked Laval to decline on his behalf, saying that he was very grateful for the Prime Minister's intention, but he could not accept it and was very sorry. Prime Minister Doumergue left the Prime Minister's office at 7:30 PM, saying that seeking opinions on the cabinet reshuffle had come to an end tonight. (14th Havas Telegram)

Death of Former French President Poincaré 46

The Savior of the Franc Falls, State Funeral to be Held on Saturday

(Paris) Poincaré, the former great President of France, known as the "Savior of the Franc," passed away this morning at 3:30 AM due to illness. (Havas dispatch, 15th)

(Paris) At the time of Poincaré's death, only family members and his closest friends were at his bedside. His passing was unexpectedly swift, even doctors did not anticipate it. Poincaré had been partially disabled since undergoing surgery in 1929. However, when he returned to Paris from his country villa three weeks ago, he seemed in good health, able to meet with friends and continue dictating his autobiography. Poincaré was deeply saddened by the Marseille massacre on Tuesday and suddenly felt unwell last night. He called for a doctor, who said there was no cause for concern and decided to visit again this morning. However, he suddenly collapsed this morning and passed away at 3:30 AM. It is expected that the government will hold a state funeral for him. (Reuters dispatch, 15th)

(Paris) It is hereby decided that the state funeral for Poincaré will be held on October 20th. His remains will be laid in state at the Martyrs' Shrine until the funeral. French Prime Minister Doumergue will deliver the eulogy at the burial, which will take place in the Poincaré family cemetery in his hometown of Sampigny. (Reuters dispatch, 15th)

(Paris) Shortly after the news of Poincaré's death spread, condolences poured in from around the world. The British monarch also personally sent a telegram of condolence to French President Lebrun. Flags have been lowered to half-mast in London. (Reuters dispatch, 15th)

Poincaré's Last Appearance

Poincaré was one of the great figures in modern French politics. He occupied an important position in French politics before the European War, during the war, and even in the ten years after the war, just like Prime Minister Clemenceau. He served as Prime Minister for two terms after the European War, and resigned in late July 1929 due to illness, at the age of sixty-nine. He was first elected as a member of parliament in 1886, and from then on, he never left his political career. Until 1929, he served the country for a total of forty-three years. Poincaré was born on August 20, 1860, in Bar-le-Duc, Meuse. His father, Antoine (first name) Poincaré (last name), graduated from the École Polytechnique in Paris and worked as a bridge and road engineer. The great French mathematician Henri (first name) Poincaré (last name) was his cousin. Poincaré studied at a local middle school in his youth, and then went to the famous Lycée Louis-le-Grand in Paris. After graduating, he studied law at the University of Paris, and then entered the Faculty of Arts, obtaining a Bachelor of Arts degree in 1878. In 1879, Poincaré, at the age of thirty, was drafted into military service and assigned to the 26th Infantry Regiment in the western French region of Rennes. After completing his military service, he obtained the qualification of a reserve second lieutenant in the Alpine Chasseurs. He began practicing law on December 20, 1883. He won his first speech victory in 1883. In 1886, Agriculture Minister Develle appointed him as the chief secretary of the ministry. After 1888, he entered the Meuse Provincial Council and became the chairman of the council the following year. He was then elected as a member of the Chamber of Deputies by the business community and always maintained a moderate attitude. He was re-elected in subsequent elections and later became a Senator of the Progressive Party in Meuse. In the National Assembly, he served as the rapporteur for the budget. In 1893, he served as the Minister of Education, and later served as a cabinet member several times. In 1912, he served as the Prime Minister, and he was responsible for the negotiations with Germany over the Moroccan issue at that time. On January 17, 1913, he was elected as President by a vote of 429 to 327. When the European War broke out, Poincaré was in St. Petersburg, the capital of old Russia. On July 29, 1914, he rushed back to France and immediately mobilized the army. Poincaré was at the forefront of the French army's initial failures and the victory at the Marne. During the four years of the war, Poincaré constantly inspected the front lines, carefully observed the changes in the situation, and personally participated in the command of the war. Poincaré's hometown was Lorraine, which was lost during the Franco-Prussian War. Throughout his life, Poincaré was always wary of Germany. After the armistice on November 11, 1918, he rushed to Alsace-Lorraine to comfort the people and was delighted to see the restoration of the homeland. On January 10, 1920, he ratified the Treaty of Versailles. The National Assembly immediately declared that Poincaré had made great contributions to the country. On February 18, 1920, he left office after his term as president expired. He then became a Senator, and from 1922 to 1924, he served as Prime Minister again. At that time, Germany was unwilling to comply with the peace treaty. Poincaré worked hard to force Germany to fulfill its responsibilities. At the same time, there was speculation on the French franc. Poincaré reorganized the financial system and stabilized the French currency. The fact that the French franc is still a stable currency in the world today is due to Poincaré's efforts. It is not without reason that the French people regard Poincaré as the "Savior of the Franc." On May 11, 1924, after the re-election of the Chamber of Deputies, the Radical Socialist Party won a major victory. Poincaré resigned on his own initiative due to the change in the majority party in the National Assembly. However, he made a comeback in 1926 and organized a national unity cabinet to rectify the situation, just like the "Party Truce Cabinet" organized by Prime Minister Doumergue this time. In that year, France faced financial difficulties. Poincaré made the National Assembly pass a bill to reduce government spending, open up tax sources, and establish a public debt consolidation bureau to clear up the finances. For a time, the foreign exchange rate of the French franc rose and the financial situation greatly improved. He then signed the world-renowned Briand-Kellogg Pact. On July 27, 1929, his body was weakened and he could not bear the heavy work. After being advised by doctors, he resigned and went into retirement. After undergoing surgery, he gradually recovered. In June 1930, he returned to the Senate. In the winter of that year, his old illness recurred, and he retired to Sampigny or Paris, and did not hear about political affairs until now. He was elected to the Académie française in 1909 and often went in and out of the hospital. He has written extensively on history. Poincaré called it "Serving France." (Havas dispatch, 15th)

Slovenian Party Leader Tearfully Appeals to the People

The capital of Yugoslavia. After the assassination of the Yugoslav King, the entire Yugoslav people feel more spiritually united in the midst of adversity. Investigation into the Marseille Case Reveals the Truth 48

The Assassin's Nationality Confirmed as a Member of a Terrorist Group

The Assassination Aimed at Transforming the Yugoslav State

The capital of Yugoslavia. The true name and origin of the assassin who assassinated the King, who claimed to be Kalman and also Suke, has now been revealed after investigation. The person's real name is Vlada (first name) Georgieff (last name), also known as Chernozemsky, a Bulgarian, born in the mountains of Macedonia, Kamenica. Georgieff is well known in the Macedonian terrorist party. It has now been proven that the appearance of the Marseille assassin is identical to that of Georgieff. Georgieff had participated in several assassinations by the Macedonian "Ohrana" Revolutionary Party. In 1913, he was the personal chauffeur of "Ohrana" party leader Mihailov and was later used as a messenger, traveling between the "Vasdačist" group's operational center in a certain foreign country and Petrich. Petrich is Mihailov's headquarters in Bulgarian Macedonia. (Havas dispatch, 14th)

Dispatch from the capital of Yugoslavia. The Marseille massacre is generally believed to have been initiated by the terrorist group "Vasdačist." The terrorist group believed that after the assassination of King Alexander, the Kingdom of Yugoslavia could be immediately disintegrated and rebuilt into an empire, including Austria, Hungary, and the Croatian people of the Yugoslav state. (Havas dispatch, 15th)

Belgrade. It was officially announced here today that the assassin of King Alexander was Vlada Georgieff, a Bulgarian, who was the chauffeur of Ivan Mihailov, a famous leader of the Macedonian terrorist party. He used many aliases. The most recent registered name was Petre Les Kalimen, which was also the name on the forged passport. Now that the assassin's true name has been confirmed, the international police are now engaged in investigating the entire terrorist party and its assassination plot. (National dispatch, 15th)

The Ministry of Colonial Affairs' Attitude Weakens 50

(Tokyo) Although yesterday was Sunday, the top officials of the Ministry of Colonial Affairs still held a meeting at the official residence of the Minister of Colonial Affairs to draft a rebuttal statement against the Army's statement on the Manchurian institutions issue. At 6:00 PM, Vice-Minister Tsubouchi, Bureau Chief Ikomawa, and Bureau Chief Kitajima visited Prime Minister Okada and Minister of State Kawada Han at the Prime Minister's official residence to explain the content of the draft rebuttal statement and requested understanding. The content of the recommendations is generally as follows: The Kwantung Government officials oppose the reform plan, not because of misunderstanding, but because of their belief in carrying out national policy in the best possible way. The main points of their opposition are the following three: (1) Appointing the Commander of the Military Police as the Chief of the Police Department; (2) Placing military officers in the Police Department; (3) Military police infringing on the duties of police officers, etc. In short, it is only to clarify the distinction between civil and military rule. Therefore, future countermeasures cannot be limited to improving the administrative structure, but the most important point is to obtain the support of the people. It is believed that it is necessary to devote oneself sincerely to this end. (Den-tsu dispatch, 15th)

(Tokyo) The Ministry of Colonial Affairs issued a proposal last night, and the Ministry of the Army is unwilling to refute it. However, its opinions are generally as follows: It is said that the Army and the Ministry of Colonial Affairs are in conflict and contention. Therefore, the Army does not want to refute the Ministry of Colonial Affairs' proposal. The proposal is a recommendation from all the officials of the Ministry of Colonial Affairs to the Minister of Colonial Affairs, which is an internal matter of the ministry. The original reform plan has already been passed by the cabinet, and Prime Minister Okada, who is also the Minister of Colonial Affairs, has also expressed his agreement. Now it cannot be changed. Two Section Chiefs Submit Resignations 51

(Tokyo) Mori, the Planning Section Chief of the Ministry of Colonial Affairs, and Hatta, the Police Affairs Section Chief, submitted their resignation letters to Okada, who is also the Minister of Colonial Affairs, today because of their anger at the dispute over the reform of institutions in Manchuria and their sense of responsibility for the local opposition to the cabinet-approved plan. The submission of the resignation letters of the two section chiefs caused a great shock to the entire Ministry of Colonial Affairs, and criticism of the top officials, including Vice-Minister Tsubouchi, has risen sharply. Given this situation, a collective resignation of the entire Ministry of Colonial Affairs may be difficult to avoid. The higher-ranking officials below the two section chiefs also seem likely to carry out a collective resignation because of their anger at the weak attitude of the top officials. Therefore, its progress is worth noting. On the other hand, non-commissioned officers, in order to encourage the higher-ranking officials, gathered in the conference room at noon today to create a resolution and hand it over to the higher-ranking officials. Therefore, the situation is deeply worrying. (Den-tsu dispatch, 15th)

(Tokyo) Tsubouchi, the Vice-Minister of Colonial Affairs, and Okada, who is also the Minister of Colonial Affairs, discussed the case of the resignation letters submitted by Section Chiefs Hatta and Mori on the afternoon of the 15th. As a result, they refused to accept them and decided to return the resignations of the section chiefs. (Nichiren dispatch, 15th)

Kwantung Police Officers' Declaration 52

Judging from the actual situation in Manchuria and from the perspective of implementing the Empire's national policy, we believe that the most perfect plan is the one proposed by the Ministry of Colonial Affairs, and we firmly believe that it will win the support of the Empire's public opinion. However, the government shattered it, leaving no trace. However, the imperial police officers who are responsible for maintaining peace and security in Manchuria and protecting the interests of the nation cannot stand by. It is deeply unexpected that some people are instigating the implementation of arbitrary politics in a corner of Manchuria and Mongolia. We will resolutely reject it. We will uphold the spirit of national construction, embody the will of the successive emperors, expand the responsibilities of civil and military affairs, and strive for unity through the co-prosperity of Japan and Manchuria, and build a world of peace and happiness. Therefore, we will move forward towards the goal we have been pursuing. (Den-tsu dispatch, 15th)

Hishikari's Mediation is Hopeless 54

(Changchun) Director-General Hishikari made a final report to the government regarding the reform of institutions in Manchuria. Director Nakamura and Director of Documents, Mizutani, arrived in Changchun at 7:30 PM yesterday. They immediately visited Director-General Hishikari at the embassy. Director Nakamura presented the overall intention of the Kwantung Government officials, which is that the government must adopt one of the following three options: (1) The government takes responsibility for the decision to make an unreasonable reform plan; (2) Fundamentally change the reform plan; (3) Postpone the implementation. One of the three must be chosen, otherwise the current state of disarray among the Kwantung Government officials cannot be resolved at all. Therefore, Director-General Hishikari's appeasement and mediation can be regarded as definitely hopeless. After the meeting, Director Nakamura told reporters that he was very sorry for Director-General Hishikari, but judging from the current situation, if the government does not choose one of the above three, there is no way to solve the problem. Moreover, the basis for the Army's statement that the Commander of the Military Police should concurrently serve as the Chief of the Police Department is very weak. (Den-tsu dispatch, 15th)

Tensions Rise in US-German Relations After Announcement of Treaty Abolition 56

Germany Refuses to Pay Full Dawes Debt Interest

US Government Accuses Germany of Discrimination

(Washington) The commercial and economic relations between the United States and Germany are gradually becoming tense after the German government announced the termination of the US-German commercial treaty at the end of last week. In addition, Germany also stated that those who hold Dawes bonds from the United States will only be able to receive three-quarters of the interest due today. The situation has become even more serious. Although official criticism has not yet been issued, it is understood that the US government believes that the proposal to reduce the Dawes loan interest is simply discrimination against the United States, as Germany will still pay the full interest to those who hold Dawes bonds from the other seven countries. The abolition of the most-favored-nation commercial treaty is inconsistent with the policy of Secretary of State Hull. Hull advocates the expansion of most-favored-nation treatment and the removal of international trade barriers. Therefore, the State Department is quite cold to the German Ambassador Dr. Luther's suggestion to begin negotiations to revise the commercial treaty. The current US-German commercial treaty will remain in effect until October 13 of next year. (Reuters dispatch, 15th)

British Air Race 57

To Begin on the 20th of This Month

Pilots from Around the World Report

(London) Crowds gathered at the Mildenhall airfield in Suffolk, England, today to see the arrival of famous pilots from around the world, as the air race between London and Melbourne will begin on the 20th of this month. All participating pilots must report today. A total of twelve aircraft arrived today, including seven British, two New Zealand, and one each from Denmark, Australia, and the United States. In addition, there are two aircraft each from the United States and the Netherlands. Because the aircraft are very large, they have already reported in Martlesham. It is reported that nine aircraft have been granted an extension to report. However, two of these nine aircraft are still in the United States and it is doubtful whether they will be able to participate on time. There are also two Italian aircraft that have not yet arrived, but if they arrive in Mildenhall within the next few days, they will be allowed to join the competition. Therefore, the final list of participants has not yet been finalized. It is estimated that about twenty-three aircraft will depart from England on October 20. The famous British pilots Mr. and Mrs. Mollison will also join the race at that time. They will use a twin-engine "Comet" monoplane, which was specially made by the de Havilland company. Its construction and contents are currently kept secret, but it is known that it can fly 2,000 miles with a full tank of fuel and has a maximum speed of 200 miles per hour. Among the US participants is Pangborn, who made a non-stop flight from Japan to the United States in October 1931, and Polando, who flew directly from New York to Istanbul in 1931. The Royal Aero Club of the United Kingdom is responsible for taking care of the race from the United Kingdom to Kupang, while the Melbourne Air Race Committee manages the area from Kupang to Melbourne. Traffic and observation matters throughout West Malaysia have been arranged, and pilots can receive assistance at any time. Police, doctors, public works personnel, and Boy Scouts have all taken on rescue duties. Telephones and wires have been installed everywhere to meet the needs of the pilots. Hourly weather reports are also published at various key points for the participants' reference. It is expected that the participants in this race will all be long-distance, fast planes, and most will fly directly from Allahabad in India, across a thousand miles of sea, to Singapore. (Reuters dispatch, 14th)

Sa Fojun Discusses the General Situation of the European Railway Industry 58

(Nanjing) Sa Fojun, the Director of the Railway Department, who was sent to the United States this spring to investigate railway engineering in various countries, has returned to Nanjing. According to him, the most important thing I was ordered to investigate was railway steel rails, water-land transport terminals, and station projects. I left the country in March and went to the United States first. Our country's steel rail standard is 85 pounds, while the standard weight of the latest rails in the United States has increased to 150 pounds, a difference of almost double. However, after investigating in European countries, most still use 90- to 95-pound steel rails. However, the railway industry in Europe and the United States is no longer what it used to be. Business is declining and income is decreasing period by period. The main reason is the development of roads and their fierce competition with railways. Currently, travelers in countries with good roads prefer to drive cars rather than take trains. However, governments are still making great efforts to maintain railway operations. Recently, various countries have paid great attention to improving the mechanical engineering of trains, so there has been considerable success. The United States now has the latest streamlined trains running in New York, Germany has the Hamburg Flyer, France has invented the Beaumont train, and the Netherlands has the Hord diesel-electric train. Their forms are different from ordinary trains, they are lighter in weight, and their speeds are extremely high. A study report is currently being drafted. (Special dispatch, 15th)

October 15th, Reuters Special Commercial Report

Gold and Silver ▲London Gold Price This morning, the gold price rose four and a half pence to one hundred and forty-three shillings and one pence.

Spot price was 67 rupees and 4 annas, November futures were 67 rupees and 5 annas, and December futures were 67 rupees and 8 annas.

Exchange Rate The London foreign exchange market did not see the authorities using the equalization fund to adjust market prices this morning. The pound continued to weaken in the morning. The exchange rate between British and American currencies opened at 4 yuan, 9 jiao, and 075, which was one pound lower than the closing price of British and American currencies on Saturday. ▲New York The prices plummeted at the opening today, falling by 45 pounds. The decline continued in the morning. The price at the time of reporting was five pounds lower than the opening price.

Letter to the Editor Zhang Taiyan's Letter 101

I read in your newspaper on the 15th a special dispatch from Beiping on the 14th, stating that "Zhang Taiyan arrived in Beiping today and will stay briefly before returning to Shanghai," etc. I have been lecturing in Suzhou recently and have not left my door for a single step. The Singapore Naval Base in the Eyes of the British 102

For Defending Australia from Japanese Invasion

Does Not Advocate Interfering with the Japanese Invasion of China

Singapore Special Correspondent The Singapore is the naval base of the British Far East Navy. The importance of its position was stated in my previous communication, and I think readers can remember it. The Singapore-based Sunday Times published yesterday another airmail special communication from London, dated September 12th, which excerpted a text recently disclosed by British government figure Sir Russell in the naval military record. This article not only provides a frank explanation of the position of Singapore in the future world war, but also clearly expresses the British position on the United States and Japan. Sir Russell also said that "Britain does not need to interfere with the Japanese invasion of China, but should protect British interests in China and exchange conditions with Japan," which further shows the British attitude towards Japan, which is very important to us. I have therefore translated the main points below for the reference of my compatriots in the motherland.

Sir Russell's original text first analyzes the composition and utilization of a huge naval base. It is said that the use of a new-style naval base is actually more than just a convenient facility for accommodating warships. There are many convenient harbors that can accommodate large ships in the Pacific, and there are many that belong to Britain. However, there is a big difference between peacetime and wartime. The construction of a new naval base is mainly due to political and military considerations. It is also said that the Singapore naval base at the tip of the Malay Peninsula is not designed to deal with any country, but is intended to defend and prevent any country from using naval power to deal with any British territory and disrupt British trade. But in reality, defense also depends on real strength. If this kind of strength is used for aggression, it becomes an aggressive force. But what will be the attitude of the aggressor? This is not usually predictable. They secretly plant their amazing power while maintaining the appearance of peace and friendship, but they are always ready to attack. In the Pacific, the countries known as naval powers are the United States and Japan. Our peace politicians will exclude the United States from the targets of war, because it is unthinkable to fight against the United States. However, I have never seen any remarks from the United States that it is unthinkable to fight against Britain. On the contrary, the United States has a lot of discussion, comparing the British Navy as a target for shooting. This is truly an open and unfriendly attitude. Not long ago, a high-ranking official in the Japanese political world made a statement about the attitude that country has adopted towards China. That kind of statement was too shocking, and major American newspapers headlined "We must act in concert with Britain." I feel that this headline is very noteworthy, because the degree of understanding between us and the so-called high-level newspapers in the United States is too poor. Everyone can guess the idea behind the above-mentioned American newspaper's request, because the American Navy's request is to enable the United States to effectively exert its own goals without acting jointly with any country. Secondly, the American newspaper then discussed the possibility of Singapore being used, saying that the Japanese government exchanged a conciliatory attitude, saying that the diplomats who made the declaration were not authorized to speak by the Japanese government, and what they said was misunderstood. This statement aroused further anxiety in the United States, and the anxiety caused to Britain by this statement was less than that of the United States. Although Japan explained it, it still could not explain the doubts of the United States, so the resumption of diplomatic relations with Russia was promoted by this. Because Russia itself has no way to deal with Japan's naval power, but if Russia and the United States unite, then Russia's Vladivostok will be able to serve as a base for the American fleet, but this hope can only be realized if the American fleet can arrive there first. Singapore is too far from Japan. When a war breaks out between Japan and China, Hong Kong is vulnerable to severe attacks. This may be the reason why Britain proposed at the Washington Conference that it would not build fortresses and equip armaments in Hong Kong, but would exchange the construction of a naval base in Singapore. However, the purpose of building a port in Singapore is clearly an appropriate interception position for Japan's naval advance towards Australia. The islands in the Pacific entrusted to Japan's rule are often regarded as defensible submarine bases, but these islands have no hiding places and are not easy to defend. If they are attacked by air, it will be very difficult to resist. However, if Japan is at war with any naval power, it may be possible to defend as much as possible, but it is not known. In my (Russell himself) view, that kind of war will occur in the period when Japan acts against China without regard to the intervention of the powers. Once the war begins, no strong country in the world can use its own power to expel Japan from the Chinese territory, because Japan will place its battleships in the inland sea of ​​China, and at the same time use its fleet to maintain traffic. I do not think that expelling the Japanese naval fleet from the Chinese territory is a matter for our British people. If the League of Nations carries out the League Covenant in a sacred manner and orders the British fleet to carry out this task, then the Geneva Palace of Peace will soon close its doors, because this kind of event is not our responsibility. If we are not so crazy and chivalrous, then we may be able to sign the first treaty with "Manchukuo", and our merchant ships will not have to stick to it and let them rust and rot, but this is another theory. Japan's inevitable initiation of a world war is as undoubtedly certain as the sun will rise tomorrow, but what we hope is that when Japan launches it, it will not take the shortcut of finding a new world position in British territory. If China cannot concentrate its full strength to resist due to pirates and bandits, even though Britain has huge trade interests in China, I have not seen that Britain should come out to interfere. Japan will exchange the protection of British trade interests in China for Britain's non-interference. The purpose of the United States is, in any case, to consider its own interests. The United States may once again oppose Japan's further aggression against China, but I must repeat this statement, the United States is considering its own interests. The real task of the Singapore naval base is to strengthen the strength to safeguard British territorial interests. This kind of interest does not require us to cooperate with other powers. If we cooperate with other powers, the responsibilities we bear will be beyond the original plan.

Looking at the above-mentioned remarks of Sir Russell, we can know that the time for coordination between Britain and the United States is still far away, and the concept of Britain's pro-Japan is still very strong. What is the background of Britain's recent dispatch of a European industrial inspection team and our country's failure to be elected to the League of Nations Council? Sharp-eyed people should be able to see it.

Chiang Kai-shek's Visit to Luoyang 103

Attending the Opening Ceremony of the Military Branch School

Inspecting the Ordnance Factory in Gong County

And Taking a Special Train to Xi'an from Luoyang

Luoyang Correspondence: Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, along with Zhang Xueliang and others, arrived in Luoyang. Their special train departed from Hankou at 8:00 AM on the 9th and arrived in Zhengzhou at 3:00 AM on the 10th. They immediately transferred to the Longhai Railway westward, arriving at Luoyang West Station at 10:00 AM. Zhu Shaozhou, the director of the Central Military Academy Branch School, Gao Guizi, the commander of the 84th Division, Wang Cifu, the concurrently serving county magistrate of Luoyang County, Chen Dabai, the director of the Central Plains Social Education Center, as well as He Yingqin, Liu Zhi, and others who had arrived in Luoyang the day before, and representatives from all walks of life, all came to the station to welcome them. The station platform was heavily guarded by soldiers of the 84th Division and county police. Chiang Kai-shek alighted from the train amidst the strains of military music and exchanged brief greetings with the welcomers before proceeding by car to the Military Academy Branch School in Xigong to attend the opening ceremony. The details are as follows:

The opening ceremony of the Xigong Central Army Military Academy Branch School was originally scheduled for 9:00 AM on the 10th, and a National Day celebration was to be held at the same time. However, due to the late arrival of Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's special train at 10:00 AM, the entire body lined up on Zhongzheng Road to welcome him. The opening ceremony was then changed to 11:00 AM. After Chiang Kai-shek arrived at the Xigong Military Branch School and rested briefly, he immediately held a military review. Besides the 2,000 officers and training class of the Military Academy Branch School and the sergeant instructors, there were also two regiments of the 84th Division stationed in Luoyang. The large parade ground in front of Guanghan Palace was extremely lively at that moment. After the commander-in-chief reported the number of personnel to Chiang Kai-shek, Chiang immediately rode a black steed with Zhang Xueliang, He Yingqin, Liu Zhi, and others, and inspected them for a week, then held a march-past. The troops were full of spirit, and Chiang Kai-shek, Zhang Xueliang, and others praised them greatly. After the review, Chiang Kai-shek first gave a speech, roughly saying that in commemorating National Day, we must not forget the martyrs who died during the revolution. After He Yingqin and Zhang Xueliang finished their speeches, a luncheon was held. At 2:00 PM, he attended the opening ceremony of the Peace Elementary School attached to the Military Academy Branch School. Chiang Kai-shek first went to the school, toured around for a week, guided by Zhu Shaozhou, and asked in detail about the school's construction process. Then the opening ceremony was held. Chiang Kai-shek first gave a speech, roughly saying, "Children, today is October 10th, hence the name 'Double Tenth.' We are all people of the Chinese nation, and the Republic of China was born today, so we are all here to celebrate it today. Who gave birth to the Republic of China? It was our Founding Father, Sun Yat-sen, so when we commemorate National Day, we must firmly remember our Founding Father, Sun Yat-sen." Finally, he encouraged the children of the school to be filial to their parents, respect their teachers, and become good citizens in the future. Afterwards, a photograph was taken. At that moment, Madame Chiang Kai-shek, Soong Mei-ling, arrived from the city, and Zhu Shaozhou immediately greeted her at the entrance. After Madame Chiang arrived at the meeting place, she sat beside Chiang Kai-shek, and another group photo was taken. At 3:00 PM, a special party branch of the Military Academy was established. Chiang Kai-shek personally came to give a speech, detailing the significance of establishing the party branch. Next, He Yingqin gave a speech, urging the military academy to work on three points for the party. Finally, Wang Chaofan, a central representative, gave a speech as the supervisor of the election. After the ceremony was over, Chiang Kai-shek and his wife took the same car back to the special train headquarters at the West Station.

On the 11th, at 8:00 AM, Chiang Kai-shek, accompanied by Zhang Xueliang, He Yingqin, Liu Zhi, and others, took a special train to Gong County Ordnance Factory for inspection. At 11:00 AM, Chiang Kai-shek and Zhang Xueliang took the same special train back to Luoyang. He Yingqin took the Longhai Railway's special express train, passed through Zhengzhou, and returned to Nanjing, reportedly staying in Nanjing for a few days to handle affairs of the Ministry of Military Administration before going to Shanghai to pay respects at the mourning of He's mother-in-law, Madame Wang. Liu Zhi got off the train at Sishui, inspected the county's administration, and then went straight back to Kaifeng. Chiang Kai-shek's special train returned to Luoyang West Station. At 2:00 PM, he and his wife took a car to the Luoyang Zhougong Temple Central Plains Social Education Center for inspection. The center was sponsored by Dai Jitao and Niu Yongjian, the two presidents of the Examination Yuan. When repairing the Zhougong Temple, Chiang Kai-shek had donated a large sum of money. After Chiang Kai-shek arrived at the center, he was led by Chen Dabai, the director of the center, to inspect the Dingding Hall, the Stele Forest, and other projects, and visited the public reading room, public school, Luojing Park, and other places. Chiang Kai-shek and his wife greatly admired the beauty of the center's environment. After the inspection, they returned to the headquarters. That night at 11:00 PM, they took a special train to Xi'an with Zhang Xueliang. Secretary-General Yang Yongtai and others followed.

Chiang Kai-shek stayed in Luoyang for two days. In addition to attending the opening ceremony of the Military Academy Branch School and inspecting various places, He Yingqin, Liu Zhi, and others gave detailed reports on local defense. It is said that Chiang Kai-shek will also visit Kaifeng after inspecting Xi'an (12th).

Sixth Route Army Captures Gulonggang 104

The Pseudo Eighth Army Corps Has Already Collapsed

Ningdu and Xingguo Will Be Taken Soon

Nanchang Correspondence: Gulonggang is located in the north of Xingguo and runs parallel to the county towns of Ningdu and Xingguo. To the south is the main road to Yudu and Ruijin. The bandits regarded Gulonggang as important in the central part of southern Jiangxi, so they deployed the newly formed pseudo Eighth Army Corps, Zhou Kun's 22nd, 23rd, and 24th divisions, and the Xingguo Yongfeng Independent Regiment to build fortifications in sections in the area west of Xingguo and south of Yongfeng, to prevent the National Army from advancing south. However, the Sixth Route Army, advancing south from Yongfeng Longgang, gradually built bunkers towards Gulonggang, opened roads, and advanced south in sections. The divisions of Ou Zhen and Liang Huasheng fought dozens of battles, large and small, and completely destroyed the bandit's fortifications on the dangerous mountains from Longgang to Pinghu. On the 7th, they attacked the positions of the pseudo 21st and 23rd divisions entrenched in Tianzisheng, Fengche'ao, Fenshui'ao, and Lotus Mountain. Starting on the 9th, they used infantry, artillery, and air force to attack the bandit positions again, taking a three-sided encirclement. On the morning of the 10th, they captured the bandit nest of Gulonggang. The entire pseudo Eighth Army Corps collapsed and fled to Qingtang Mountain in Ningdu. The National Army is still following up. Gulonggang is only twenty or thirty miles east of Ningdu. The Sixth Route Army's victory here, together with the Third Route Army advancing west from Shicheng, has formed a pincer attack. The bandits in Ningdu will be cut into two pieces by the Third and Sixth Route Armies. The situation of Xingguo City being surrounded on three sides has also been formed. Therefore, the capture of Gulonggang is a prelude to the capture of the two county towns of Ning and Xing. The connection between the bandits in Ning and Xing counties has also been cut off, and their disintegration is imminent. (October 12th)

Wuxi Textile Industry Appeals for Exemption from Increased Consolidated Tax 105

Telegram Sent to the Executive Yuan and the Ministries of Finance and Industry

Wuxi Correspondence: The local Cotton Textile Industry Association, having heard that the government intends to implement an increase in the consolidated tax from November 1st of this year, convened an emergency meeting yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM. It was resolved to immediately draft and send telegrams to the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of Industry, and the Shanghai Cotton Control Committee, appealing for exemption from the increase. The original text reads: "Recently, we heard news of an increase in the consolidated tax on cotton yarn. The rumors are spreading, and the industry is alarmed. The association's Shenxin No. 3, Zhenxin, Qingfeng, Guangqin, Lixin, Yukang, and Fuxing factories, due to the dumping of Japanese goods and the decline of the rural economy, are on the verge of bankruptcy. On July 17th of this year, we sent a telegram appealing for a reduction in the consolidated tax, but it was not approved. We are still in a state of anxiety when shocking news arrived that the government is planning to increase taxes. This is tantamount to strangling the dying and hastening its death. We recently read reports that the Shanghai Chinese Yarn Factory Federation and the Hubei Branch have sent telegrams appealing for relief. The factories of the association, being located inland, feel the pain of the great depression of yarn factories in recent years even more acutely. If the government truly intends to increase taxes, we earnestly request that you consider the deep pain and wounds of the domestic cotton textile industry, which can hardly bear any further burden. Please immediately cancel this proposal; otherwise, the livelihood of the manufacturers will be destroyed, and the government's tax revenue will also dry up. Both will suffer. The factories of the association, under urgent and pressing circumstances, are sending this telegram to beg for mercy. If our request is not granted, we will have no choice but to suspend operations and await orders. We pray earnestly, hoping for your consideration. Tsai Chien-san, Chairman of the Wuxi County Cotton Textile Industry Association, kowtows in寒 (cold) (humble)." (15th)

The home of Wu Youlan, a wealthy man in Zhu Jiahang, Punan, was robbed and looted last year, resulting in a significant loss. Yesterday, the criminal court of the county court sentenced Xia Dasan and Mazi Xia San to twelve years of imprisonment each, and Zhou San to three years of imprisonment.

Taicang

Convicted Robber Gong Asong Executed by Firing Squad 108

On May 4th, 1932, the case of Zhang Hui Gao's family, a villager in Zhintang Township, being robbed and shot, was investigated by the Public Security Bureau, and three suspects, Zhou Asi, Jun Shaoyun, and Gong Asong, were arrested one after another. After separate investigations, the facts were clear, and they were sentenced to life imprisonment. Gong Asong escaped twice during his sentence and then committed robberies and injuries, accumulating crimes. He was arrested this time, sentenced to death, and approved by the superiors. Yesterday afternoon, the prisoner Gong Asong was tied to the execution ground and executed by firing squad.

The Taicang Restaurant, located at No. 205 Zhonghe West Road in the city, suddenly caught fire around 2:00 AM this morning. In an instant, the flames burst through the roof, and the situation became uncontrollable. By the time the neighbors heard the alarm and sought help, the restaurant building had been completely destroyed. The Zhenxing Clothing Store and the Wanchunyuan Teahouse suffered the most severe losses, with total losses estimated at over ten thousand yuan, which was a great stroke of luck amidst the misfortune.

The county government here, in order to implement the use of the new system of weights and measures, specially invited grain merchants from the five counties of Wuxi, Kunshan, Wujiang, Wujin, and this county yesterday (15th) to a meeting to discuss the date of changing to the new system. Zhao Zixin from Wuxi, Chen Junyu, Zhou Hongqing, and Xu Jusheng from this county, and representatives from Jiang, Kun, Chang, and other counties, totaling more than twenty people, attended. Local Bandits Rob Farmhouse 113

Yao Shuangfu, a resident of Yinjiazhuang near Huangtutang in the Sixth District of the county, is a farmer who leads a relatively comfortable life, which attracted the attention of bandits. Around 2:00 AM the day before, twenty to thirty local bandits suddenly arrived, with white cloths wrapped around their heads, each holding iron rulers, wooden sticks, flashlights, and other weapons. They broke down the door and entered. Yao's wife, Wu, carrying a child, hid on the roof. Shuangfu obtained a gong and also escaped to the roof to sound the alarm. The bandits realized that things were not going well and immediately pulled out fake pistols and set off firecrackers several times to show off their power. They then grabbed Shuangfu, beat him, and forced their way into the house, looting extensively. They stole cash, clothes, etc., worth about three hundred yuan.

Letter Received

Letter from the Xihulu Road Engineering Office 117

Dear Editor, I read a news article in your newspaper's Changshu Correspondence column on the 14th of this month titled "First Opening of the Xichang Highway Results in Overturn." This is not in accordance with the facts. The bridge and culvert engineering of the Xichang section of this road has indeed been completed, and the improvement of the roadbed is currently being carried out by the relevant county governments in accordance with the regulations of this office. Before the completion of the improvement project, there was no opening to traffic, nor was there any order from the department to open the road within this month. However, the United Federation of Private Electric Power Companies previously sent a letter requesting temporary opening of the dirt road on the Xichang section of the road for their annual meeting, so that members could enjoy the scenery along the way. This office responded with a formal letter stating that the roadbed was not solid and it was not appropriate to open the road to vehicles, politely declining the request. Subsequently, the annual officials of the association planned to conduct a test drive on the Xichang section of the road before it was opened to traffic. Therefore, on the 12th of this month, they hired a car to go for a test drive on their own. As a result, the wheels got stuck in a ditch and could not move forward. There was no overturning, nor were there any technology department officials present. Fearing that the rumors are inaccurate and could mislead the audience, we have written to you specifically requesting correction. Sincerely, Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department Xihulu Road Engineering Office, Editorial Department of Shen Bao Newspaper.

Six-Percent Sterling Boxer Indemnity Bonds Drawn for Redemption Yesterday Morning 121

Total of 239 Bonds Drawn for 52,000 Pounds Redemption

Payment to be Made by Central and Four Other Banks on January 1st Next Year

The first drawing of the six-percent sterling boxer indemnity bonds for redemption was held at 10:00 AM yesterday in the main hall on the third floor of the Central Bank. More than thirty representatives from various circles attended. Xu Keting, Director of the Coinage Department of the Ministry of Finance, presided over the meeting and divided the drawing into seven groups, drawing a total of 239 bonds. All winning bonds will be redeemed with interest starting on January 1st next year by the Central, China, Transportation, HSBC, and other four banks. The details are as follows:

Attending Representatives 122

Xu Keting, Director of the Coinage Department of the Ministry of Finance; Jiang Lufu, Director of the Public Debt Department; (Xia Dai) (Supervisor) Xu Jianping, representative of the Ministry of Finance; Shen Zaochi, representative of the Audit Department; Gao Weici, representative of the Ministry of Railways; (Drawers) Jin Wenyuan, Central Bank; Zhu Qizhen, Bank of China; Jin Guobao, Bank of Communications; and Zeng Rongpu, Boxer Indemnity Board; Ju Zhijing, First Special District Court; Wang Huailian, Money Industry Association; Wu Weiru, Donglai Bank; Chen Yaozu; Ren Yingzhong; Mao Shijian; Qi Xianyong; Zhang Jingli; Wang Fengsheng; and more than thirty other representatives.

Chairman's Report 123

Today, the first drawing for redemption of the six-percent sterling boxer indemnity bonds of 1934 is being held. We are honored to have the representatives from the three Ministries of Finance, Railways, and Audit supervising, and the representatives from the various organizations visiting, and the banks accepting the bonds providing valuable assistance. I would like to briefly report on the issuance and drawing of these bonds. These bonds were jointly issued by the Ministries of Finance and Railways, with a fixed amount of 1.5 million pounds sterling and an annual interest rate of six percent, for the purpose of completing the Guangdong-Hankou Railway. The funds for redemption and interest payment are from the Boxer Indemnity returned by the British to the Ministry of Railways (domestic portion), which is allocated monthly and kept by this committee. Interest and principal will be paid twice a year, on January 1st and July 1st, for a total of twelve and a half years. The order of redemption will be determined by drawing. January 1st, 1935, is the date for the first redemption, and the drawing will be carried out today. All drawing methods and procedures have been printed into a booklet with detailed explanations, which will be distributed on the spot and will not be repeated. I will now begin the drawing. The supervisors are requested to first examine the same two copies of each of the 1,000 bonds, put them into the drawing drums, and then apply them alternately and draw in rotation.

Drawing Procedures 124

The chairman explained that first the 50-pound bonds will be drawn, then the 100-pound bonds, and then the 1,000-pound bonds. There are 68 50-pound bonds to be redeemed this time, one bond per draw, so 68 draws should be drawn, divided into two groups, with 34 draws per group. Each group has 1,000 bonds, which are loaded into the barrels. An average of 3 draws is conducted in each barrel, for a total of 30 draws. There are still 4 draws to be added to a barrel. 10 additional labels were prepared. Before the drawing, the added barrel number was first drawn. The chairman asked the supervisors to check the 1,000 labels of the three-digit number labels of the first group. The labels should be pre-divided into 20 editions with 50 labels per edition arranged neatly for inspection. After the ticket number in the ticket log of the first group has been verified, the supervisors will store the labels in 10 barrels in order, 100 labels per barrel. The chairman requested the supervisor to check the barrel labels and immediately draw the additional barrel labels. The supervisor will verify and then draw the additional 4 barrel labels. The reporting staff will report to the chairman and announce it on the spot. This time, 1 label each will be added to the 1st No. 1-whatever number barrel, No. 2-whatever number barrel, No. 3-whatever number barrel, and No. 4-whatever number barrel, which are sent to the record seat for registration. The chairman requested the drawing staff to take turns drawing in turn, for a total of 34 draws. The drawn labels will be reported to the chairman by the attendants and announced on the spot, i.e. which number won, and sent to the record seat for registration separately, and written on the blackboard. After the first group drawing is completed, after each group drawing is completed, the drawn label number is written on the blackboard, and the attendants must put the drawn labels back into the original barrel for sorting. After the first group drawing is completed, the barrel labels and the second group labels and the label register should be sorted and prepared for inspection. The number of wins and win certificates recorded in the subsequent group label book will be sent to the chairman and all the members, and the supervisor for review, and the certificate will be signed and sealed.

Silver Export Tax Collection Started Yesterday 126

This can prevent a large outflow in the future.

However, attention must be paid to the development of international trade.

A Central News Agency report states that since the U.S. government raised the price of silver to buy existing silver, a large amount of silver has flowed out of our country, which has had a significant impact on social finance. The silver and money industries and other four associations in this city have paid close attention to this and have petitioned the Ministry of Finance to increase the silver export tax to prevent this. This has been approved and implemented yesterday. Because the matter arose suddenly, about 9 million yuan that had already been loaded onto ships yesterday were returned. The details are recorded below:

Implemented Yesterday 127

The increased silver export tax rate was approved by the Ministry of Finance and was instructed to the Customs Administration the night before last (the 14th) to be implemented yesterday. After receiving the order, the Customs Administration immediately forwarded it to the Inspector General of Customs, as well as to the superintendents and commissioners of all customs houses, to comply with and handle accordingly. The Jianghai Customs, due to the urgency of the matter, did not have time to make a public announcement yesterday. However, the Minister of Finance, Mr. Kong Xiangxi, convened a meeting of Chinese and foreign bankers in this city at his residence on West Adams Road the night before last and explained the measures for increasing the export tax.

Calculation Method 128

The tax rate formulated by the Ministry of Finance: (1) Silver standard currency will be subject to an export tax of 10%, minus the minting fee of 2.25%, resulting in a net tax of 7.75%. (2) Large bars of silver will be subject to an export tax of 10%. (3) The equalization tax will be calculated based on the difference between the ratio of the London silver price and the Shanghai exchange rate and the exchange rate determined by the market on that day. If the payment of the above export tax is still insufficient, it will be made up. At 11:30 AM yesterday, the Central Bank announced the equalization tax to be 4.75%. The calculation method is as follows: The London silver price of 24 and 3/8 pence last Saturday is multiplied by the statutory number 8165744, and the sum is 1 shilling and 7 pence and 15/16, minus the Shanghai market price of 1 shilling, 5 pence and 3/4 at 11:30 AM that day. The difference is 2 and 3/16 pence, which is equal to 12.5%, minus 7.75%, which means that the equalization tax to be levied is 4.75%. Therefore, the tax to be levied on silver coins is 12.5%, and the tax to be levied on fixed silver is 14.75%.

Silver Reserves 129

After the sudden implementation of the silver export tax yesterday, those who had already loaded goods onto ships but had not cleared customs returned them one after another. According to the Customs' announcement yesterday, a total of 9.25 million yuan of silver was returned, including 8.52 million yuan in silver dollars and 730,000 yuan in silver bars, mostly loaded by foreign banks onto the President Grant and the Kalheshlin ships for shipment to the United States. Therefore, foreign banks expressed surprise at the Chinese government's swiftness in implementing the tax increase. As for the city's silver reserves, on the 2nd of this month, there were 52,610,000 taels of silver, of which 22,880,000 taels were held by Chinese banks, 346,510,000 yuan in silver dollars, of which 243,600,000 yuan were held by Chinese banks, and 7,980 silver bars, all owned by Chinese banks. On September 26th of last year, the silver reserves were 137,495,000 taels and 298,780,000 yuan, of which 45,360,000 taels and 179,120,000 yuan were held by Chinese banks.

Official Statement 130

According to a senior member of the banking community who spoke to reporters, the Ministry of Finance's implementation of the silver export tax increase can prevent the continued large-scale export of silver and stabilize public confidence. However, after implementation, it can only prevent the outflow of silver caused by the U.S. raising the price of silver. Our country has always been a country with an import surplus, so it is still inevitable that silver will flow out due to the difference in international trade. In the future, people must pay close attention to the development of international trade. Our silk and tea industries' international trade has failed, and the reason lies in the fact that our merchants do not understand the market conditions and social needs of various countries. Therefore, people must first investigate the needs of various countries and develop exports, so as to offset imports and exports and avoid the outflow of silver.

Inauguration of the Central Cotton Watering and Adulteration Prohibition Office 131

According to the National News Agency, the National Economic Commission's Central Cotton Watering and Adulteration Prohibition Office, after the appointment of Liu Weizhi, the permanent vice minister of the Ministry of Industry, as the director, and Ye Yuanxin as the deputy director, was established at 113 Jiujiang Road. Yesterday was the official opening day of the office. Chen Guangfu, the chairman of the Cotton Industry Control Committee of the National Economic Commission, specially invited all committee members to participate. Those who attended included Chen Guangfu, Zhang Gongquan, Bei Songsun, Liu Weizhi, Ye Yuanxin, Guo Shun, He Bingxian, Nie Lusheng, Tang Shenghai, Li Shengbo, Xu Caicheng, Zou Bingwen, Chen Bozhuang, Mu Ouchu, etc. After the ceremony, Chen Guangfu first delivered a speech on behalf of the Cotton Control Committee, followed by a reply from Director Liu Weizhi, a report on the preparatory work by Deputy Director Ye, and finally a speech by Mu Ouchu. The speeches of each person are recorded below: (A)

Chen Guangfu's Speech 132

He said, "Today is the inauguration day of the Central Cotton Watering and Adulteration Prohibition Office. Director Liu Jisheng attaches importance to pragmatism and does not want extravagance. Therefore, today's inauguration ceremony is held only within our association's regular meeting. The participants are also limited to the members of this office. As for the opinions to be expressed to the outside world, Mr. Jisheng has indicated that he will choose another date to hold it after taking office. The malpractice of cotton adulteration has a history of at least 50 years in China. Since the establishment of this committee in October last year, we have formulated four major guidelines for improving our country's raw cotton plan. In short, (1) Improve and increase the quality and quantity of cotton production nationwide to offset the import of more than 100 million yuan of foreign cotton each year, and even establish cotton production, transportation, and sales cooperatives to organize our country's cotton farmers and promote the committee's plan to improve cotton production nationwide. At the same time, we will also communicate with financial institutions so that municipal funds can help cotton farmers improve cotton production. (3) Train cotton grading personnel and send them to various cooperatives to conduct cotton grading so that cotton nationwide can gradually be graded using scientific methods to seek fair treatment in trade. The above matters have been handled by the Central Cotton Improvement Institute, as well as the cotton watering and adulteration problems in Shaanxi, Henan, and Jiangsu provinces. This matter requires the Legislative Yuan to pass the prohibition regulations and the Executive Yuan to pass the detailed rules for the implementation of the prohibition regulations, so it will inevitably be delayed. Therefore, the Central Cotton Watering and Adulteration Prohibition Office can only be established today. Among the provinces that have established provincial prohibition offices, there are Henan and Shaanxi. Hubei, Hebei, and Shandong provinces will soon be established. The prohibition business in Jiangsu Province will be handled concurrently by the Central Prohibition Office. According to the detailed rules, Shanghai City should be handled by the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau. Other cotton-producing provinces, such as Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, and Hunan, have all sent people to contact and are in preparation. What is particularly admirable is that this time, the committee's implementation of the prohibition of cotton watering and adulteration is not only a joint effort by the central and provincial governments, but also yarn merchants and cotton merchants across the country can uphold the government's intention to improve the cotton industry and obey the orders carefully. The Ministry of Industry presides over the national industry. Today, Vice Minister Liu Jisheng is specially appointed as the director of the Central Cotton Watering and Adulteration Prohibition Office of this committee, which shows its importance to this matter. This cannot but be specially thanked to the Ministry of Industry on behalf of this committee. Finally, Guangfu has a word to tell the gentlemen of this committee, that our country is the most suitable country for cotton production. If the improvement and promotion are done in the right way, not only can the import of raw cotton worth hundreds of millions of yuan be reduced, but also the eastern neighbor, Japan, purchases American and Indian cotton every year, with a value of more than 900 million Japanese yen, which can be regarded as the best market for our country's export of raw cotton. All efforts are needed, and prohibiting cotton watering and adulteration is also one of the efforts to be made. Fortunately, Mr. Liu Jisheng and Mr. Ye Yuanding are in charge of the director and deputy director of the office. The members of this committee have unlimited hope. On the day of the establishment of the office, on behalf of this committee, I pay tribute to Mr. Liu and Mr. Ye. (B) Director

At the same time, I serve in the Ministry of Industry, so since I have been recommended by the Cotton Control Committee, I cannot refuse. Now that our country's cotton watering and adulteration prohibition work is handled in this way, we will definitely get good results in the future. For the country to improve production, it will definitely get good results if it continues to be implemented for two years. Under the guidance of the Cotton Industry Control Committee and with the deputy director having a lot of experience in cotton production, I will naturally follow everyone's efforts and work hard.
