If we want to eliminate this national disaster, it cannot be done in a day or two, so we have to rely on today's youth, especially educated youth. If we want to rely on youth, we must restrain and discipline them without getting discouraged, so that they can become organized and disciplined citizens to shoulder the heavy responsibility of defending and saving the country. Nowadays, all countries in the world, whether in politics, economy, or military, are centered on national defense. The future war will require total mobilization of the entire country. Our country boasts of its vast territory and abundant resources, but 450 million people are unorganized, undisciplined, and untrained. How can we drive them to fight? Although the resources are abundant, they cannot be developed and manufactured. Raw materials cannot be made into products. What use are they? Therefore, President Chiang Kai-shek advocates the New Life Movement to militarize the people of the whole country to achieve this goal. European and American countries underwent major transformations after the Industrial Revolution a hundred years ago. Our country is still dreaming today. It is truly fortunate that we have not perished immediately. But we cannot regard luck as a principle. If we cannot make efforts to carry on the past and open up the future, the country will perish on our shoulders. Therefore, we should bear the responsibility for the rise and fall of the country. If we work hard, the country can be revived. If we do not work hard, the country will definitely perish. I hope everyone will work hard.

▲ Director's Talk: After the ceremony, they gathered in front of the City Government Auditorium and took a group photo with Mayor Wu, Director Pan, and others to commemorate the occasion. They then went to the Municipal Education Bureau, where Director Pan gave a talk, roughly stating: (1) When you go to serve in various schools, because many schools do not fully understand, many difficulties will definitely arise. Therefore, we recently convened a meeting of school principals to break through these difficulties. (2) Currently, many schools cannot provide salaries according to the standards promulgated by the Ministry due to financial difficulties. Some schools have relatively higher salaries, and there is a great inequality in treatment. We are also thinking about how to make the instructors in various schools have the same treatment. (3) Military training is not only about teaching students to attend classes and drills, but also about training students to be organized, disciplined, and fond of group life. Therefore, we will suggest to the Central Government in the future that military instructors in various schools should also serve as trainers. After the talk, everyone returned, and Director Jiao convened a luncheon before everyone returned to their schools.

The Chinese Industrial and Commercial Management Association, recently due to various opinions, all believe that the greater reason why Shanghai's industry cannot compete with other countries is the lack of management talents. Now, in order to remedy this shortcoming, the association, in conjunction with the Mechanical Engineering Association, has specially established an industrial management training class to study the practical problems of management within factories. The preparatory situation of the class is briefly recorded below:

▲ Training Class Outline: (1) Auditors: Any staff of factories or those who aspire to study industrial management can attend, but the number is limited to 60. (2) Instructors: Experts who have long been researching management are hired to serve as instructors. (3) Tuition: Each person pays three yuan. If sent by the factory, it is free. (4) Training Time: Tentatively set for three months, every Wednesday from 7:00 pm to 9:00 pm. (5) Address: Inside the Chinese Industrial and Commercial Management Association, 146 Hardoon Road. (6) Opening Date: Scheduled for October 17.

▲ Course Objectives: (1) Production Management: Purchasing and management of principles, management of machinery, implementation of work, inspection of products, management of goods, transportation issues. (2) Accounting System: New-style accounting and improved old-style bookkeeping, cost accounting, improvement of accounting system. (3) Personnel Management: Organization and authority, selection, training, allocation, wages, benefits, meetings, cooperation, labor union issues, etc. Distribution problems, advertising, investigation, sales, agency system, credit sales, collection issues, etc.

Publication of "How to Use the Library" 195

The library undertaking in our country has been quite developed in recent years, but specialized works on library science are still rarely seen, especially those that guide users in how to use the library. In view of this, the editor of this book, Mr. Lu Shaoyu, a lecturer at Great China University, has specially compiled this book based on his research insights and experience to serve as a guide for those who use libraries. The contents are divided into eight sections: 1. The Structure of Books, 2. The Arrangement of Books in the Library, 3. Card Catalogs, 4. Dictionaries, 5. Encyclopedias, 6. Other Reference Books, 7. Reader Guidance, 8. Bibliographies, etc., which are very practical.

Personal Views on Implementing Production Education (Part 4) 196

▲ Speech by Mr. Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Municipal Education Bureau, at the General Meeting of Members of the Third District Education Association in this City

How to guide primary and secondary school students towards the path of production? In other words, how to make them have interest, knowledge, skills, and habits in production? The most important thing is that the teachers who teach the courses in general primary and secondary schools are willing to take responsibility. If they can take production as the center of the primary and secondary school curriculum, teaching materials, teaching methods, and training goals, design methods of reform, implement them through experiments, and then promote them, then it will not be difficult for teachers to lead primary and secondary school students onto the path of production. Many people say that teachers teach different subjects. Teachers who teach mathematics, physics, chemistry, biology... teachers in science subjects, and teachers who teach crafts, and agricultural and industrial subjects, are close to nature and can of course lead students to production. However, teachers who teach civics, Chinese, social studies... teachers in humanities subjects, only know how to teach students to read, write, study, and compose essays, and read history and geography, which have nothing to do with production skills. Speaking of this, I want to mention teaching materials. I believe that the current teaching materials really need fundamental reform. A few days ago, I went to a primary school in the countryside of Jiangwan Township to inspect, and I saw fifth and sixth grade students taking history class, talking about the Crusades. The Crusades certainly had an impact on the spread of world culture, but it may not necessarily have much to do with the children in our Chinese villages. What is called the Crusades? Why did they want to go on an eastern expedition? Can the teacher explain it in detail? Can rural children of eleven or twelve years old understand it? They can't even figure out the several dynasties in Chinese history, but they have to memorize foreign names such as Alexander of Macedon. What exactly is going on? Taking the Crusades as an example, the dispute between Christianity and Islam, the establishment and destruction of the Kingdom of Jerusalem, the success and failure of the seven or eight eastern expeditions, and the impact on the communication between Eastern and Western cultures, etc., can be taught in universities, and long lectures can be compiled. Orally, it can be at least one or two hours, and students can take notes of hundreds or thousands of words. This is a historical fact with a lot of material, but in primary school textbooks, everything is included in only two or three sentences. I ask, which teacher has the ability to use only two or three sentences to make children around ten years old understand the Crusades? They will inevitably read it once according to the book, and it is good enough if the children can remember it. What relationship does this kind of teaching material have with the children's own lives? Therefore, when we talk about history, we should pay attention to the relationship with the primary and secondary school students themselves, and we should pay attention to production. For example, first talk about the local history of a certain place, the evolution of production technology in the local area, and then the production capacity and production methods of the Chinese nation, how it was before, how the annual evolution is, and whether it is progress or degradation now. For example, Shennong taught people how to cultivate, Leizu taught people how to raise silkworms, the well-field system of the Three Dynasties, Shang Yang's abolition of field boundaries... these are all historical facts related to people's livelihoods, and should be specifically brought up in advance, so that students can know how our ancestors produced and improved in the past... how precious production is. If so, although history is taught, the history he teaches is very relevant to production. Similarly, those who teach Chinese can also adopt materials about production, such as narrating the material selection and methods of carpenters making tables and chairs, describing the feelings of seeing cotton in the fields during suburban travel, visiting yarn factories, etc., announcements of recruiting workers, donation appeals for purchasing water-lifting machines... On the one hand, they teach them to read and write articles, but on the other hand, they have practical uses, giving primary and secondary school students a very important impression of production. It cannot be said that it has nothing to do with production. Since this is the case, why not imitate the current unit design of primary schools and always use "production" as a consistent teaching material center in primary and secondary schools? In addition, the distribution of courses is also very important. If we follow the current course distribution of primary and secondary schools, I am afraid that students, especially children in primary schools, will feel that there is no time to do production experiments and labor work, because there are too many subjects and the amount is too heavy. Therefore, if we believe that production education is the path to take in the future, then we should ask teachers to make a determination to thoroughly transform the selection of teaching materials and the allocation of courses.

A few months ago, I had some ideas about this issue of teaching materials and courses, and now I will tentatively put them forward as a reference. I believe that teaching materials should be selected as the central teaching materials only after careful and objective screening in the children's life tendencies. Our curriculum is "the whole life" and should also implement "production education" in "life." In primary schools, we must oppose the past compartmentalized teaching method with its heavy workload, because children's psychology is different from adults. What they need is not a rigid classroom life of lecturing and talking about metaphysics, but interesting activities. Teachers should always guide children's interests and satisfy their desire for knowledge. For example, children like to raise chickens and raise organisms, and they all have the nature of asking questions. They must be wondering how they were born, why they were born so beautifully, what to feed them, what is the use of them... Then they will ask the teacher to give them a satisfactory solution. This is the beginning of the motive for designing and doing schoolwork. Later, you can teach him to actually feed them, read stories about chicks, calculate the value of feed and the amount of eggs laid, write the words "chicks eat white rice," play the game "hawks catch chicks," sing the song "little chicks"... These many things start from the motive of raising chickens and continue until the children's desires are satisfied. It is not to instill knowledge into children for no reason. It is always the need of the children's own lives, which also indicates the path of production to them. It is learning from doing, teaching from doing, it is real learning, it is real teaching, and it is a method of learning and teaching with the spirit of design, so that children can gain interest, knowledge, skills, and habits in production from actual life. This is "production education" in primary schools. (To be continued)

International Track and Field Games Postponed to Next Spring 198

It is already late autumn and all countries are unprepared.

A meeting of representatives from various countries for the Shanghai International Track and Field Games was held at the Shenyuan Football Field yesterday (the 14th) at 5:30 pm. Those present were Huai Lun (British Army), Ke Fen (British Army), Huai Xu (British), Si Huohua Dun (American Mailings), Hao Er (Xiqing and Haiqing), Bai Naite (American), Jiang Xiangqing (Chinese), Rong Qizhao (Chinese), Zhang Guoxun (Chinese), Le Xiurong (Chinese), Agoye de (French Army). The meeting was chaired by Mr. Shen Siliang, the executive of the Association. After reporting the reasons for the meeting, the date of the current Games was discussed. The representatives believed that the time was already late autumn, and that the countries were not adequately prepared. Rather than rushing to complete it in this inappropriate period, it would be more appropriate to postpone it to next spring. Therefore, it was decided by a majority vote to postpone this Games.

Two Railway Bureaus Sponsor International Student Climbing Competition 207

At this time of year when the autumn is high and the air is crisp, and the weather is good, the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureaus are using the holidays to promote climbing, exercise young people's bodies, and encourage the interest in travel. They have launched the Mogan Mountain Shanghai Student International Climbing Competition. The starting date is set for 3:00 pm on October 20th, starting at Yucun and ending at the main entrance of the Mogan Mountain Railway Hotel, a distance of eight kilometers. Any young person aged 16 to 25 with a certificate from the school authority, regardless of gender or nationality, can participate in the competition. The quota is at least 20 people and at most 80 people. During the competition, they will be divided into male and female groups. The first place in each group will be awarded a silver cup, the second place in each group will be awarded a silver shield, and the third place in each group will be awarded a large silver medal. The school with the highest score among the participating students will be awarded a pennant, a commemorative flag, and a commemorative mirror. All other participants will be given a commemorative medal. The registration deadline is October 15th. It is reported that the two railway bureaus have sent circulars to secondary and above schools in this city to solicit participants and also welcome guests from all walks of life to watch the competition. Those who wish to participate in the competition or watch the competition can register with the Shanghai North Railway Station Chief Station Master's Office, the Jing'an Temple Road First Business Office, or the Nanshi Second Business Office.

The Impact of the Silver Tax Increase 210

Since the silver tax increase was implemented yesterday, the market has seen a sudden impact, with the most severe being the standard gold. The opening price immediately rose by 19 yuan and 1 jiao (927.5), and the highest was 930 yuan and 8 jiao. As a result, it rose by 9 yuan and 7 jiao. Yarn prices also rose by 1 yuan and 5 jiao, and flower prices rose by 3 or 4 jiao. Public bonds also saw an upward trend in the initial session, but in the end, as soon as there was a rise, there was an outflow, and the market was difficult to rise. Coarse sand and white sugar also rose, but the actual sales were stagnant, and the rise was very small. The rise in flour and wheat was even more crazy. Finance

Silver Tax Increase Causes Bullion Price to Rise by 9.7 Yuan 211

Spot Premium Still Flat, Difficult to Trigger a Squeeze

Market Sentiment Initially Firm, Then Weakens

Yesterday, the gold market surged after the Chinese government announced an increase in the silver export tax to 7.75%, along with a requirement to make up the difference in exchange rates to balance the tax. This move would prevent banks from exporting silver, ensuring that silver would no longer flow out of the country. Due to exchange rate issues, banks lacked capital, causing panic among short-selling Chinese merchants. The foreign exchange market became extremely tight, stimulating the gold market, and causing bullion prices to rise. However, November contracts are based on foreign exchange rates, while December contracts will be based on a new pure gold settlement standard, which will be greatly affected. Moreover, the November contracts are approaching their rollover date. Therefore, although the gold market rose, it was not strong enough, and the underlying trend was quite flat and weak. The market opened with pre-market bids at 927.2 yuan, with very bullish sentiment. Short sellers rushed to cover, and the price rose to around 930 yuan in a blink of an eye before slightly falling. After the official opening, short sellers continued to cover, and the domestic market was extremely tight, once approaching the 930 yuan mark. However, after the Central Bank announced its exchange rates, with the British pound flat and the US dollar down only slightly by 0.1875, the new standard had no impact. At the same time, those holding long positions in November contracts took advantage of the high prices to sell, gradually falling by more than 9 yuan. Some in the market said that the new tax was a trial run for two weeks. When the HSBC exchange rates were announced, with the British pound down 0.0375 and the US dollar down 0.0875, the foreign exchange market became even tighter. Chinese merchants continued to cover, struggling because banks had no appetite to sell, so the price rebounded. In addition, the swap premium rose to around 6 yuan, and buying suddenly became strong, breaking through the 930 yuan mark. However, supply suddenly increased at the high prices, and the price gradually fell, but still struggled. Later, as the swap premium became cheaper, market sentiment also turned weak, and large players also started to sell and move to spot positions. The public's attention shifted significantly. With the deadline for November contracts approaching, many long positions were rolled over, and the spot premium dropped to 1 yuan, causing the gold market to fall again. At noon, with the spot premium still stable, the Central Bank announced that a balanced tax of 4.75% would be levied today, and the domestic market was still difficult to cover. After a period of weakness, it turned slightly stable. The market was stable in the afternoon, but the swap premium gradually fell, and market sentiment turned from stable to weak. Despite large players buying, supply exceeded demand, and the price gradually fell. Although there was a struggle at the 920 yuan mark, the overall trend was still weak. There were rumors that the new tax rules still faced obstacles. In reality, the only major short seller left was Zhengchang, who had already largely moved into the December contracts. Most retail short sellers had already covered, making it difficult to stir up buying. Finally, although the price fell due to a sharp rise in silver, it was still able to rebound after the drop. The market situation was chaotic throughout the day. With November contracts approaching rollover and the Central Bank's exchange rates being relatively small, market sentiment was not very bullish. The swap premium was between 2.1 and 2.7 yuan in the market. There were rumors that the Central Bank was occasionally opening spot positions. The market situation for the day is recorded below.

The market opened at 927.5 yuan in the morning, up 19.1 yuan from last Saturday, and the foreign exchange market suddenly became extremely tight. Ruixing, Tongyi, Dachangxiang, and Jintiao rose from 7 yuan to 9.8 yuan. HSBC's January forward price was 0.9375, while Hengyu, Fuxing, Yongdingkang, and Dadecheng's forward price fell to 4 yuan. Dadecheng slightly bought at the low price, suddenly rising to 5.5 yuan. Yuankang, Xiangfuxing, and Yongfulai sold, and the price fell again to 1.5 yuan. The Central Bank's forward exchange rate remained unchanged. HSBC's announcement of the British pound falling by 0.0375 and the US dollar falling by 0.0875 was anticipated. Fuchang, Yuansheng, Yongqing, Yuyuan, Yuyong, Zhaofengchang, etc. bought one after another, gradually rising. Banque Belge covered December US dollars at 0.0625, and the price rose to 7.8 yuan. Hengyu, Fuan, Zhaofengchang, Dalianbang, Dafa Yong, etc. continued to sell, and the price fell again to 5.8 yuan. The swap premium was expected to rise to around 6 yuan, and market sentiment improved. Brokers aggressively covered December US dollars at 0.05625, but failed. Then, Banque Belge covered January US dollars at 0.04375. Yicheng, Hengyu, Zhaofengchang, Yuansheng Yong, Fuan, and Tongchun bought repeatedly, and the price rose to 930.08 yuan, mainly because the swap market was firm. Mitsui sold December US dollars at 0.0375. Hengxing, Dalianbang, Hengyu, Fuxing Yong sold, and the price fell to 926.6 yuan. Yuanyi Fuxing Yong bought at the low price and then rebounded to 928.7 yuan. After entering the afternoon, the swap premium became smaller and smaller, and market sentiment also weakened. Yuanyi, Hengyu, Qingyu, Qianchangxiang, Yuanyong Hongxing, etc. jointly sold, and the market became oversupplied as long positions were closed, gradually falling. Although there was some support in the middle, Dadecheng suddenly sold, and the market's attention shifted. The spot premium once fell to within 1.5 yuan, and the gold market also fell to 921.4 yuan. Hengyu and Dadecheng bought contracts at low prices, and general short sellers also rushed to sell. The swap premium rose, and the gold price rebounded to 925.8 yuan. Shunmao, Yuanyong Bingxing, etc. sold, and the price fell again to 923.3 yuan. Yuanyong bought contracts at low prices, managing to maintain the price. At noon, the market closed at 923.4 yuan. After the market closed, the trend rebounded, once rising to around 925 yuan.

The market opened at 924.8 yuan in the afternoon, and market sentiment was weak, falling from 925 yuan. The swap premium fell again to 2.5 yuan. Hengyu Yuanchang Yong Yuanchun sold contracts, falling to 1 yuan. Yuqing Yong Yuanyong Tianfeng bought at low prices, rising to 3.5 yuan. Mitsui sold January forward contracts at 0.0875. Banque Belge bought December US dollars at 0.075. Dadecheng Hengyu sold contracts, and Futaiheng, Dachangxiang, Yuqing Yong still bought, and there was still a struggle. Later, Hengyu Dadecheng Fuxing Yong Yongfeng Fuchang came to sell, and the price fell to 919.5 yuan. Hengxing Yuanyong bought contracts at low prices, rebounding twice. However, market sentiment was weak, and retail long positions sold, gradually falling from outside 921 yuan to within 920 yuan. 120,000 Bags of Foreign Rice Newly Arrived 218

丨丨Market Prices Also Rise by Two Jiao丨丨

Yesterday, the market for foreign white rice generally trended upwards. Due to the gradual depletion of stocks in the market recently and the limited number of arrivals, the low prices of foreign rice futures led to a surge in market sentiment. Speculators and hoarders, coupled with the implementation of the silver tax, which is bound to raise prices, caused foreign rice to rise sharply by two jiao, and white rice by varying amounts from a few fen to more than a jiao. The entire city handled 1,200 bags of white rice and 3,795 bags of foreign rice from this street, and 726 bags of white rice and 600 bags of foreign rice from the interior. The sharp rise of two jiao in foreign rice was not entirely due to the silver tax. It was mainly because the two ships originally scheduled to arrive in Shanghai at the beginning of last week were delayed en route for several days. The floating stocks in the market were depleted, and the owners hoarded their goods, which, coupled with the silver issue, led to a sharp rise of two jiao. The futures market for October opened at 300 tons, with initial sales in the morning at 4.75 yuan. In the afternoon, due to the activity in the spot rice market, the price jumped up by one jiao to 4.85 yuan. The two ships of foreign rice, with no fixed arrival date, arrived completely yesterday. However, they will need to be unloaded and go through customs inspection procedures, so the goods will not be available for delivery for at least three to five days. These two ships are the Talay Sima La, carrying 50,000 bags of Italian rice, and the Milly Mara, carrying about 70,000 bags of rice, totaling about 120,000 bags. However, this cargo was originally sold in September and will mostly be used to cover futures contracts. Therefore, although the number of arrivals is large, there is not a large floating stock in the market.

Chronicles

Little Western Paradise 220

— By Zhang Henshui

Chapter 3: Pitying a Lost Girl Peeking Through the Door; Cherishing Jade and Visiting a Poor Family to Hear of Hardships

Li Shilian asked: "Is there Western food here?" The waiter replied: "Yes! Many division commanders and brigade commanders from outside invite guests here. Foreigners who come to Xi'an always stay here because we specialize in Western food. I don't see anything special about Germans eating Western food, but they drink too much beer. They drink beer like water, a whole glass at a time, and they don't drink tea all day." Zhang Jiefu heard that Germans drink beer like that, and his throat vibrated, and he stretched his neck, as if he had already swallowed a mouthful of phlegm. Cheng Zhiqian looked clearly into the lighted rooms from outside the window, and couldn't help but smile secretly. Turning his head, he saw a Westerner typing at a table in a small courtyard across the way, the typewriter rattling, and he didn't even look up. This was probably the German that Zhang Jiefu was talking about. He thought, what is this German doing here? I'll have to investigate tomorrow. Cheng Zhiqian wandered under the eaves for a long time, and then he added two things to worry about. After breakfast the next morning, he saw two Caucasians testing the engine of a car in the large open courtyard, making a loud noise, so he took the opportunity to come out and wanted to talk to the Caucasians. Just then, the waiter brought in a woman with bound feet. She walked holding the door frame, smiling and whispering, "Is it that room?" Saying that, she looked back. And shouted, "Come on! Didn't you want to see the foreign houses? Come on!" He shouted several times in a row, and a girl of sixteen or seventeen years old walked in from outside the courtyard door. As soon as she saw someone, she lowered her head, held the door, and hesitated to enter. The waiter said, "It doesn't matter, just go in. There are foreign-style cave dwellings built in the back, and there are large foreign buildings in the front. You can see them all." The girl probably also had a sense of curiosity. After the waiter boasted like this, she entered the door. (40)

New Suggestions for the Double Ninth Festival 221

— By Qifenglou Master

Social customs, once established for a long time, become deeply entrenched and difficult to reform in a short period of time! The "moon viewing" and eating "moon cakes" of the Mid-Autumn Festival have already passed with much fanfare. Now that the Double Ninth Festival has arrived, everyone remembers the "mountain climbing" and eating "Double Ninth cakes." However, having witnessed the current situation, I would like to offer some small suggestions for these two activities. Although it involves games, it does not hum the slogan "Entertainment should not forget saving the country," so I think it is harmless.

▲ Change Mountain Climbing to Airplane Riding The story of mountain climbing is that Huan Jing had a disaster on the ninth day of the Double Ninth Festival, and Fei Changfang ordered his whole family to wear dogwood pouches and climb the mountain to avoid the disaster, thus escaping the misfortune. However, now looking around the country, it can be said that disasters and famines are everywhere, and thorns fill the path. Even the mountaintops and watersides may be affected! Therefore, the only way to avoid disaster is to take an airplane and fly straight into the clouds, soaring in space, or perhaps avoid it by one in ten thousand.

▲ Eating Cake Should Be Changed to Eating饼 "Liu Lang dared not write the word cake, falsely bearing the name of a great poet," this refers to the story of Liu Mengde writing poetry on the Double Ninth Festival. As for when the eating of Double Ninth cake began, I am sorry that I cannot answer. However, every year on the Double Ninth Festival, cake is eaten every year, and as a result, the current social situation has become so terrible! In this sluggish economy, why not change the pattern this year and eat cake instead? Because there is only the saying "too cake," but never "cake cake," and cake is round, which can also be said to imply a sense of completeness. Eating it may give the hope that incomplete things will be reunited.

The spirit of resisting goods has weakened, and imported shark fins have majestically ascended to the table. A gourmet said: "The country is what I love, and shark fins are also what I love. The two cannot be had at the same time, so I will give up the country and take the shark fins."

On a Pedal Boat 223

— Baling

I sat on a pedal boat to go to a relative's house in the interior, which gave me endless thoughts.

It is a small wooden boat, with a green canopy on top and pointed ends. The boatman uses oars to stir the water waves, and then the small boat gradually moves forward. This is the "pedal boat" that is about to be eliminated but has not been eliminated in the interior.

It is said that the business of pedal boats was still very good twenty or thirty years ago. Later, the shipping industry gradually flourished, so people enjoyed a higher level of life and everyone liked to take steamers instead of welcoming the pedal boats. Therefore, the passengers in the boat are still some old people, and farmers and peasant women who like to save a few cents. Young lads are reluctant to take this pedal boat unless they have no other choice. Therefore, the owners of the pedal boats have suffered a blow in their lives and gradually feel the "difficulty of living."

"That's right, material culture is advancing day by day, pedal boats have overthrown sailboats, and steamers have overthrown pedal boats. It seems that the elimination of pedal boats is a certain truth," said an old passenger. "But, I think: after the elimination, how will the lives of the general boatmen be solved? Isn't this going to become a problem?"

Now, the people who run pedal boats have also risen up to fight. They have also installed machines on the boats, called "machine pedal boats." Of course, using machines to drive is indeed much faster, but the number of pedal boats in the interior that can afford to install machines is really as rare as stars in the morning. So many pedal boats that cannot afford to install machines are inevitably eliminated in the end.

Alas, I sat on a pedal boat to go to a relative's house in the interior, which gave me endless thoughts.

Self-Expression 225

— Xi Tongchu

Generally, people say that children's self-expression is the strongest. In fact, if you examine the behavior of adults, their self-expression is no less than that of children. Here are a few examples:

▲ Brother Old K He is my colleague, and because his face is just like the Old K on the playing card, he is called Brother Old K. He claims to like watching movies very much. He comes back at 11:30 every night, walking so hard that the floorboards almost jump up, and everyone is awakened from their sleep. Then he criticizes how the film is in terms of consciousness, and at the same time passes the brochure to everyone. However, according to several colleagues, the brochure was obtained when he was seen passing the theater and going in to get it. He also likes to eat candy. While chewing, he gesticulates in front of you. However, the total amount he eats in a day is only what you see.

▲ Li Er Probably he is the second child in his family, so his old classmates call him Li Er. As soon as he sees you on the road, he rattles on and on about his triumphant events, over and over again. When you impatiently want to say goodbye, he turns to other things. Sometimes he deliberately calls a rickshaw and scolds the driver before sending him away. Sometimes he steps into a food company and tastes some of this and some of that. As a result, he doesn't make any deals. These are all the tricks he uses to show you.

▲ Mr. Jin Mr. Jin was an old colleague of mine when I worked at a certain school. He was really like a child. Once, he ran from a long way away, holding a Tangram set that he made by hand, and asked me to introduce him and the many colleagues here to it. After I introduced him, he said how difficult it was to make the Tangram set, how fun it was, like a treasure. As he spoke, he played it again. The colleagues were all laughing behind his back, because that thing really wasn't that surprisingly fun.

Records of Pervasive Incense 226

— Originally Written by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, Translated by Qin Shouou

Now this part is already so dilapidated that it can no longer be used for anything. And the Shanhai Pass, which was originally used to isolate us, is opened like a door. I am afraid that after a few decades or hundreds of years, people will gradually forget the original intention of the ancient emperors to build this Great Wall, until they forget it completely!"

Indeed, the Great Wall is gradually collapsing, especially near Shanhai Pass, collapsing exceptionally quickly, revealing a large gap; the track of the Jingfeng Railway passes through this gap very generously. As for the many materials that have collapsed? It must have taken a lot of financial resources to collect them in the past. Now, because no one is in charge, as soon as it collapses, it is taken by nearby residents as materials for building houses; even if it has not collapsed, some people steal it and dismantle it, and move it back to their own homes. It is no wonder that the Empress Dowager was filled with emotion about such a valuable ancient building being allowed to be destroyed and collapsed!

Now, the place where we are standing is the boundary line between the Chinese mainland and the three northeastern provinces. As long as we cross the Great Wall, the outside is the place where our ancestors entered the Central Plains and rose to power. I don't know what the Empress Dowager felt in her heart when she arrived at this place? She seemed to be most fascinated by the clear water of the Liaodong Bay. For two thousand years, the seawater here has washed the end of the Great Wall day and night, causing it to collapse automatically, gradually dying like an old man.

The Empress Dowager slowly moved her eyes, which were fixed on the seawater, to the several mountain peaks above; these mountain peaks were like prisoners who had been sentenced to imprisonment, chained by people for a long time, and their shackles were the Great Wall. (150)

World Oddities

— (Yingdai)

A Prolific Centenarian

In the area of ​​Bergrant, there was a prolific centenarian who had thirty-four sons, but recently he passed away, and his age was one hundred and twenty-two years. In his life, he had married four times, so there were thirty-four men and women under his knees. However, the hall full of children did not agree with him, so in such a big family, only one grandson was by his bed when he died. Because in his later years, the children died, separated, and only lived with that grandson.

Lenin's Former Residence

When Lenin is mentioned, perhaps everyone knows that he was a great Soviet revolutionary, and the Russians respect Lenin just like we respect Mr. Sun Yat-sen. In the area of ​​Samara, there is a house that was Lenin's former residence. He lived inside from 1890 to 1893. Now this house has been set up by the government as a library on the lower floor, and Lenin's relics are displayed on the upper floor. Soviet people, regardless of distance, come in droves every day to see the former residence of the leader.

A Beggar's Harvest

Madrid is the capital of Spain. The number of beggars there is unmatched elsewhere. According to official statistics, the city is full of beggars, 300,000 people a year, and they can beg for six million pounds, which are all accumulated from small amounts. Because it is too easy to get money in Spain, all the beggars are very rich. Among the beggars, some even wear silk shirts and gold watches. Beggars with such luxury may have opened a new record in the history of beggars around the world, which is unexpected by anyone!

The Decline of the Gambling City

Monte Carlo is a famous French city, and the gambling there is known throughout the world. The amount of gambling is huge, and millions of gold coins can be made in one night, which is really shocking to hear. However, since the world started to experience economic panic, the famous gambling city of Monte Carlo has also changed, and its image is declining day by day. Clubs are closing one after another, and nineteen out of ten casinos are closed, with signs of disintegration. In the past, ordinary poor boys could not even think of going to Monte Carlo and entering the grand and magnificent casinos. However, in order to save this crisis, starting from November 1st, all travelers, anyone, can enter the casino for free gambling without having to buy tickets.

The Russian Emperor's Summer Palace

Peterhof Palace is very close to Leningrad and is a famous Russian palace. The magnificence of the architecture and the richness of the decoration are unmatched, and it is indeed the crystallization of art. Now, it has been completely renovated under the leadership of the Leningrad City Council. The palace was originally built by Peter the Great, and it was extremely luxurious. All the decorations and embellishments that could be bought with money were in the palace, without exception. In the past, the emperors of Russia used it as a summer palace. After the revolution, it was converted into a museum. During the war, the Bolsheviks sent troops to guard it to prevent the destruction of this historical building, so it was able to avoid any damage, because the preparations at that time were thorough!

Live Fish in the Rain

It may be an unheard of thing to have live fish in the rain? But according to news recently received from Budapest, it is said that on a certain day in the area of ​​Darber, Hungary, many fresh fish fell down when it rained. In a storm, millions of small fish were mixed in the raindrops and fell to the ground. In a short time, the ground was full of small fish. This incident has attracted a lot of attention, and as a result, the fallen fish were sent to the Natural History Museum in Budapest for research.
